            Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa  
                           I  DUKA PAṬṬHĀNAṂ  
                                I  
                           HETU DUKAṂ   
  
                            Anulomaṃ   
         Hetuṃ dhammaṃ  paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati 
 hetupaccayā  
      Alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho  adosaṃ paṭicca alobho 
 amoho  amohaṃ paṭicca alobho adoso  Lobhaṃ paṭicca 
 moho  mohaṃ paṭicca lobho  dosaṃ paṭicca moho  mohaṃ 
 paṭicca doso   Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe        
         Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati 
 hetupaccayā  
      Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
         Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā 
 uppajjanti hetupaccayā  
      Alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho sampayuttakā ca khandhā 
 cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ   
                                                                            So R  and K  B  and S  hetudhammaṃ always  
   None of the texts collated give lobho and doso as 
      mutually conditioned  
   None of the texts collated give the excisions in this 
      con  nexion  R  has nowhere       pe       
   See above under    Only K  has bandhitabbaṃ  
  
  
  page      
                            Hetudukaṃ  
       Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho sampayuttakā ca khandhā 
 cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ       pe       Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati 
 hetupaccayā  
      Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ   Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca 
 vatthu   vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā  ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ       
 pe        
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati 
 hetupaccayā  
      Nahetū khandhe paṭicca hetū  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe 
 vatthuṃ paṭicca hetū  
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā 
 uppajjanti hetupaccayā  
      Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā hetū ca 
 cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  dve khandhe paṭicca dve 
 khandhā hetu ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca hetū ca sampayuttakā ca 
 khandhā  
         Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo 
 uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Alobhañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca adoso 
 amoho        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ        Lobhañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca moho  dosañ ca sampayuttake 
 ca khandhe paṭicca moho  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe alobhañ ca 
 vatthuñ ca paṭicca adoso amoho       pe       
         Hetuñ ca na hetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu 
 dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca hetuñ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā 
 cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  Dve khandhe ca hetuñ ca 
 paṭicca dve khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  Paṭi                                                                           R  adds  Dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā 
      cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
   S  and K  usually read vatthuṃ  B  and R  vatthu  
      B  vatthu also in accusative  
   All texts excise  To be read presumably with tayo       
      dve       dve  Cf  pp        §   with khandhā in this §  
  
  
  page      
                           Anekapaccayā                   
 sandhikkhaṇe vatthuñ ca hetuñ ca paṭicca sampayuttakā 
 khandhā  
         Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu 
 ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā  
      Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca alobhañ ca paṭicca tayo 
 khandhā adoso amoho cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  dve 
 khandhe ca alobhañ ca paṭicca dve khandhā adoso amoho 
 cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ        
 nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca lobhañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā 
 moho ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ       pe       dve 
 khandhe       pe       Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuñ ca alobhañ ca paṭicca adoso amoho sampayuttakā ca khandhā 
       pe       
      Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā        rūpaṃ chaḍḍetvā arūpe yeva nava 
 pañhā         adhipatipaccayā        paṭisandhi natthi  paripuṇṇaṃ   Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca       pe       mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  upādā rūpaṃ  idaṃ 
 ninnānaṃ         
 anantarapaccayā       
 samanantarapaccayā       
 sahajātapaccayā        sabbe mahābhūtā yāva asaññasattā        
 aññamaññapaccayā       
 nissayapaccayā       
 upanissayapaccayā        
 purejātapaccayā        
 āsevanapaccayā        dvīsu  paṭisandhi natthi        
 kammapaccayā       
 vipākapaccayā        saṃkhittaṃ        
 avigatapaccayā       
                                                                            S  ārammaṇapaccayā rūpaṃ  Chaḍḍetvā arūpe ye ca neva neva pañhā  
      B  paccayā rūpaṃ chaḍḍetvā    arūpe ca nava pañhā  
   S  Adhipatipaccayā paṭisandhi natthi paripuṇṇaṃ  Naṃ mahābhūtaṃ 
      paṭicca  Mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānan rūpaṃ idanānaṃ  
      B  Idaṃ nānaṃ  R  imaṃ nānaṃ  
   S  omits  
   B  pūre  always  
   R  dvīsu pi

                            Hetudukaṃ  
           Hetuyā nava                      sabbattha nava  
           ārammaṇe nava                     avigate nava       evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ  
                           Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
                            Paccaniyaṃ   
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati 
 nahetupaccayā  
      Ahetukaṃ nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā 
 cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  dve        Ahetukapaṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca vatthu  vatthuṃ paṭicca 
 khandhā  Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ       pe       bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ        pe       
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetudhammo uppajjati 
 nahetupaccayā  
      Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe paṭicca 
 vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho  
         Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati 
 nārammaṇapaccayā  
      Hetuṃ paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati 
 nārammaṇapaccayā  
      Nahetū khandhe  paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  
 Paṭisandhikkhaṇe        sabbe mahābhūtā        
         Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu 
 dhammo uppajjati nārammaṇapaccayā  
      Hetuñ ca nahetū ca khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ 
 rūpaṃ  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
 nādhipatipaccayā         paripuṇṇaṃ        nānantarapaccayā  
       nasamanantarapaccayā       na aññamaññapaccayā 
       na upanissayapaccayā       
         Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati 
 napurejātapaccayā  
                                                                            Cf  p        
   B  āhāraṃ utuṃ asañña  sic   R  āhāra    utu    asañña     
      S  āhāraṃ utu  
   S  nahetu khandhaṃ  
   R  na adhi   
   R  na anant   
  
  
  page      
                 Napurejātapaccayavāro  Arūpaṃ        
      Arūpe alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho        cakkaṃ 
 bandhitabbaṃ         Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho  mohaṃ paṭicca 
 lobho       pe       Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
         Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati 
 napurejātapaccayā  
      Arūpe hetuṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā  Hetuṃ 
 paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       
 pe       
         Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā 
 uppajjanti napurejātapaccayā  
      Arūpe alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho sampayuttakā ca 
 khandhā        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ        Lobhaṃ paṭicca 
 moho sampayuttakā ca khandhā       pe        Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati 
 napurejātapaccayā  
      Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā  
 Dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā   Nahetū khandhe paṭicca 
 cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati 
 napurejātapaccayā  
      Arūpe nahetū khandhe paṭicca hetū  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe 
       pe       
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā 
 uppajjanti napurejātapaccayā  
      Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā hetū 
 ca  dve khandhe       pe       Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
         Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo 
 uppajjati napurejātapaccayā  
      Arūpe alobhañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca adoso 
 amoho         cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ        arūpe lobhañ ca 
 sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca moho        cakkaṃ 
 bandhitabbaṃ        Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
         Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu 
 dhammo uppajjati napurejātapaccayā  
                                                                            Cf  p    under    S  adds dhammaṃ  
   B  and R  repeat cakkaṃ  
   R  omits sentence

                            Hetudukaṃ  
      Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca hetuñ ca paṭicca tayo 
 khandhā       pe       dve khandhe       pe       nahetū 
 khandhe ca hetuñ ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  
 Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
         Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca 
 nahetu ca dhammā uppajjanti napurejātapaccayā  
      Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca alobhaṃ ca paṭicca tayo 
 khandhā adoso amoho ca        pe       dve khandhe 
        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ        nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ 
 ca lobhañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā moho ca         cakkaṃ 
 bandhitabbaṃ        Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe       
         Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati 
 napacchājātapaccayā        pe       nāsevanapaccayā  
       pe       
         Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati 
 nakammapaccayā  
      Hetuṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā cetanā  
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati 
 nakammapaccayā  
      Nahetū khandhe paṭicca sampayuttakā cetanā  Bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ  
         Heṭuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu 
 dhammo uppajjati nakammapaccayā  
      Hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca sampayuttakā 
 cetanā  
         Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati 
 navipākapaccayā        pe        
         Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati 
 nāhārapaccayā  
      Bāhiraṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ  asaññasattānaṃ  Ekaṃ mahā                                                                           B   R  and S  na āsev   
   R  adds  nava   
   B  utuṃ asañña    na jhānapaccayā    bāhiraṃ āhāraṃ utuṃ asañña 
      sattānaṃ mahābhūte paṭicca rūpajīvitindriyaṃ    najhānapaccayā    
      pañcaviññāṇaṃ bāhiraṃ āhāraṃ utuṃ asañña namaggapaccayā    
      S  utu       asañña       na indriyapacca       bāhiraṃ āhāraṃ 
      utu       asañña indriyapacca bāhiraṃ āhāraṃ utu       
      asaññasattānaṃ  etc

                           Paccaniyaṃ                             
 bhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā  Mahābhūte paṭicca 
 kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ       pe        
       na indriyapaccayā       Bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ 
 utusamuṭṭhānaṃ  Ekaṃ  mahābhūtaṃ       pe       Mahābhūte paṭicca upādā rūpaṃ asaññasattānaṃ  Mahābhūte 
 paṭicca rūpajīvitindriyaṃ  
       najhānapaccayā       Pañcaviññāṇasahagataṃ  ekaṃ 
 khandhaṃ       pe       bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ       pe       
       namaggapaccayā       Ahetukaṃ nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca       pe       Paṭisandhikkhaṇe  bāhiraṃ 
 āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ       
 pe       
       nasampayuttapaccayā       navippayuttapaccayā       
  napurejātasadisaṃ  arūpe yeva          
       nonatthipaccayā       
       novigatapaccayā       
           Nahetuyā dve                      nakamme tīṇi  
           nārammaṇe tīṇi                 navipāke nava  
           nādhipatiyā nava                  nāhāre ekaṃ  
           nānantare tīṇi                  na indriye   ekaṃ  
           nasamanantare  tīṇi            najhāne ekaṃ  
           na aññamaññe  tīṇi                namagge ekaṃ  
           na upanissaye tīṇi                nasampayutte tīṇi  
           napurejāte nava                 navippayutte nava  
           napacchājāte  nava                nonatthiyā tīṇi  
           nāsevane nava                  novigate tīṇi  evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ  
                          Paccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
                                                                            R  omits last two sentences  
   R  omits to asaññasattānaṃ  
   S  Pañca viññāṇaṃ bāhiraṃ āhāraṃ utu       asañña       
      namaggapaccayā       hetukaṃ na hetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ       
      R  Pañcaviññāṇaṃ bāhiraṃ       
   R  omits  
   R  arūpapañhā yeva  
   So also R  
   B  and S  omit  
   B  nā aññ   S  nāññ   
   B  na pacch   
    K  nind   
  
  
  page      
                            Hetudukaṃ  
           Hetupaccayā   nārammaṇe           nāsevane nava  
           tīṇi                           nakamme tīṇi  
           nādhipatiyā nava                 navipāke nava  
           nānantare tīṇi                 nasampayutte tīṇi  
            saṃkhittaṃ                 navippayutte nava  
           na upanissaye tīṇi                nonatthiyā tīṇi  
           napurejāte nava                 novigate tīṇi  
           napacchājāte nava   
                      Anulomapaccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
           Nahetupaccayā   ārammaṇe          indriye dve  
           dve                           jhāne dve  
           anantare dve  saṃkhittaṃ        magge ekaṃ  
           kamme dve                      sampayutte dve  saṃkhittaṃ   
           vipāke ekaṃ  
           āhāre dve                      avigate dve  
                      Paccaniyānulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ   
       Sahajātavāro pi paṭiccavārasadiso   paccayavāro pi nissayavāro pi paṭiccavārasadisā  yeva pañhā   Mahābhūtesu 
 niṭṭhitesu vatthuṃ paccayāti kātabbaṃ   Pañcāyatanāni anulome pi paccaniye pi yathā labbhanti tathā kātabbā  
 Saṃsaṭṭhavāro pi sampayuttavāro pi paripuṇṇā  Rūpaṃ 
 natthi  arūpam eva   
                                Anulomaṃ   
         Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa hetupaccayena 
 paccayo  
      Alobho adosassa amohassa hetupaccayena paccayo       
                                                                            B  nahetu  
   R  na āram   
   R  omits clause  
   B  Hetupaccayā  
   B  and S  omit this title  
   R  omits  
   B   sadiso  
   K  yeva pañhāvāre mahābhūtesu  etc  Possibly the right reading is  
      yeva  Paccayavāre mahā   etc  Cf  pp         
   R  and S  kātabbā  
  
  
  page      
                           Ārammaṇavāro                            
  cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ        Lobho mohassa hetupaccayena 
 paccayo  Doso mohassa hetupaccayena paccayo  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe        
         Hetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa hetupaccayena 
 paccayo  
      Hetu  sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ 
 ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe 
       pe       
         Hetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca dhammassa 
 hetupaccayena paccayo  
      Alobho adosassa amohassa sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena

                            Hetudukaṃ  
 sandhikkhaṇe vatthu hetūnaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo  
 Purejātaṃ cakkhuṃ       vatthuṃ aniccato       domanassaṃ 
 uppajjati       dibbena cakkhunā       pe        saddaṃ 
 suṇāti       Vatthu  hetūnaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo  
         Nahetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca        
      Sahajātaṃ  purejātaṃ  Sahajāto nahetu eko khandho 
 tiṇṇannaṃ  khandhānaṃ hetūnaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca 
 rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthu hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo  Purejātaṃ cakkhuṃ       pe        
 saddaṃ suṇāti        Vatthuṃ hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca 
 khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo  
         Hetu ca nahetu  ca dhammā hetussa        
      Sahajātaṃ  purejātaṃ   Sahajāto alobho ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā adosassa amohassa atthipaccayena paccayo 
        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ        Lobho ca sampayuttakā 
 ca khandhā mohassa atthipaccayena paccayo        cakkaṃ 
 bandhitabbaṃ        Paṭisandhikkhaṇe alobho ca vatthu 
 ca adosassa amohassa atthipaccayena paccayo        cakkaṃ   
         Hetu ca nahetu  ca dhammā nahetussa        
      Sahajātaṃ       pe        Paṭisandhikkhaṇe hetū ca 
 vatthu ca nahetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo  Sahajātā hetū ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ 
 rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo  Pacchājātā hetū ca 
 kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo  Pacchājātā hetū ca rūpajīvitindriyaṃ ca kaṭattā 
 rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo  
         Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā  hetussa ca        
      Sahajātaṃ  purejātaṃ  Sahajāto nahetu eko khandho 
 ca alobho ca tiṇṇannaṃ  khandhānaṃ adosassa amohassa

                          Paccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
           Hetupaccayā  nārammaṇe  tīṇi       saṃkhittaṃ        
           nādhipatiyā tīṇi                 na magge tīṇi  
           nānantare tīṇi                 na sampayutte ekaṃ  
           nasamanantare tīṇi               navippayutte tīṇi  
           na aññamaññe  ekaṃ            nonatthiyā tīṇi  
           na upanissaye  tīṇi            novigate tīṇi            evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ

         Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko dhammo uppajjati nādhipatipaccayā        anulome  sahajātasadisā        
           nānantarapaccayā       
           nasamanantarapaccayā       
           na aññamaññapaccayā       
           na upanissayapaccayā       
           napurejātapaccayā   
      Arūpe sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā 
       pe       Paṭisandhikkhaṇe sahetukaṃ       pe

 paṭicca vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho  Sahetuke khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe       pe

      Arūpe vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ 
 khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā moho ca        pe       
 dve khandhe       pe       Paṭisandhikkhaṇe

 ahetuke khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe        yāva asaññasattā tāva  vitthāro

 paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ 
 paṭicca sahetukā khandhā

 mahābhūte paṭicca kaṭattā rūpaṃ

                           Anekapaccayā                        
         Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca       sahetuko        
      Arūpe vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ 
 khandhañ ca mohañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā       pe       
 Paṭisandhikkhaṇe sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ 
      ca paṭicca tayo khandhā  dve       pe       
         Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca       ahetuko       
      Sahetuke khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate 
 khandhe ca mohaṃ ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ  
         Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca       sahetuko ca       
      Paṭisandhikkhaṇe        dve khandhe       pe       
 Sahetuke khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca kaṭattā rūpaṃ  
         Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko dhammo 
 uppajjati napacchājātapaccayā       nāsevanapaccayā        
 nakammapaccayā  
      Sahetuke khandhe paṭicca sahetukā cetanā  
         Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ahetuko dhammo 
 uppajjati nakammapaccayā  
      Ahetuke khandhe paṭicca ahetukā cetanā  bāhiraṃ 
 āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ       pe        
         Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko dhammo 
 uppajjaṭi nakammapaccayā  
      Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paṭicca 
 sampayuttakā cetanā  
         Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca dhammaṃ sahetuko       
      Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca mohañ 
 ca paṭicca sampayuttakā cetanā  
            na vipākapaccayā        paṭisandhi  natthi   
         Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ahetuko dhammo uppajjati nāhārapaccayā       na indriyapaccayā       najhānapaccayā       namaggapaccayā       nasampayuttapaccayā

 paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā

 khandhañ ca mohañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā  dve

      nārammaṇe tīṇi                     navipāke nava  
      nadhipatiyā nava                 nāhāre ekaṃ  
      nānantare tīṇi                     na indriye ekaṃ

                           Paccayavāro                         
           Hetupaccayā                      napacchājāte nava  
           nārammaṇe tīṇi                 nāsevane nava  
           nādhipatiyā nava                 nakamme tīṇi  
           nānantare tīṇi                 navipāke nava  
           nasamanantare tīṇi                nasampayutte tīṇi  
           na aññamaññe tīṇi                 navippayutte tīṇi  
           na upanissaye tīṇi                nonatthiyā tīṇi  
           napurejāte nava                 novigate tīṇi       evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ  
                      Anulomapaccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
           Nahetupaccayā                  indriye dve  
           ārammaṇe dve                      jhāne dve  
           anantare dve                      magge ekaṃ  
           sabbattha dve                     sampayutte dve  
           vipāke ekaṃ                      avigate dve            āhāre dve  
      evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ  
                      Paccaniyānulomaṃ  niṭṭhitaṃ  
                       Sahajātavāro paṭiccavārasadiso

 Ahetukamūlakaṃ  paṭiccasadisaṃ yeva    
         Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā

 khandhā  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paccayā sahetukā 
 khandhā  
         Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko ca        
      Vatthuṃ paccayā sahetukā khandhā  Mahābhūte paccayā

  saṃkhittaṃ   
           Nahetuyā tīṇi                     na kamme cattāri  
           nārammaṇe tīṇi                 navipāke nava  
           nādhipatiyā nava                 nāhāre ekaṃ  
           nānantare tīṇi                 na indriye ekaṃ  
           nasamanantare  tīṇi            na jhāne ekaṃ  
           na aññamaññe  tīṇi                namagge ekaṃ  
            nanissaye tīṇi                   nasampayutte tīṇi  
           na upanissaye tīṇi                navippayutte  cha  
           napurejāte nava                 nonatthiyā tīṇi  
           napacchājāte nava                 novigate tīṇi            nāsevane nava  
      evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ  
                          Paccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ

           tīṇi                           nāsevane  nava

           nānantare tīṇi                 navipāke nava  
           nasamanantare tīṇi                nasampayutte tīṇi  
           na aññamaññe  tīṇi                navippayutte tīṇi  
           na upanissaye tīṇi                nonatthiyā tīṇi  
           napurejāte nava                 novigate tīṇi       evaṃ gaṇetabban

                           Kammavāro                         
 Kusalākusale niruddhe sahetuko vipāko tad ārammaṇatā 
 uppajjati  dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati  dibbāya 
 sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti  Vatthupurejātaṃ    vatthu 
 sahetukānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo  
         Ahetuko dhammo sahetukassa ca ahetukassa       
      Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ  vatthupurejātaṃ   Ārammaṇāpurejātaṃ    cakkhuṃ       pe       vatthuṃ ārabbha vicikicchāsahagatā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti  
 Vatthupurejātaṃ    vatthu vicikicchāsahagatānaṃ uddhaccasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca purejātapaccayena 
 paccayo  
         Sahetuko dhammo ahetukassa dhammassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo  
      Pacchājātā sahetukā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa 
 pacchājātapaccayena paccayo  
         Ahetuko  dhammo ahetukassa dhammassa       
      Pacchājātā ahetukā khandhā ca moho ca purejātassa        
         Sahetuko ca ahetuko ca dhammā ahetukassa

                      HETU CEVA SAHETUKA DUKAṂ   
         Hetuñ ceva  sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca  hetu ceva 
 sahetuko dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ   
 Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ   Paṭisandhikkhaṇe alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho        cakkaṃ

 ceva na ca hetu dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā

        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ        Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho sampayuttakā ca khandhā        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ

 atthipaccayena paccayo  Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ sanidassanānaṃ 
 kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo  
         Anidassano dhammo sanidassanassa ca       
      Sahajātaṃ  pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ  Sahajāto anidassano eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ sanidassanānañ ca anidassanānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ 
 atthipaccayena paccayo  dve khandhā       Paṭisandhikkhaṇe mahābhūtā sanidassanānañ ca anidassanānañ ca 
 cittasamuṭṭhānānañ        Bāhiraṃ  mahābhūtā sanidassanānañ ca anidassanānañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ upādā rūpānaṃ 
 atthipaccayena paccayo  
         Sanidassano ca       anidassanassa

 paccayo

                           Anulomapaccaniyaṃ                         
         Sanidassano dhammo sanidassanassa  dhammassa 
 ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo       upanissayapaccayena 
 paccayo       
         Anidassano dhammo anidassanassa  dhammassa

 kamma   āhāra   indriyapaccayena paccayo

 sahajāta   pacchājāta   kamma   āhāra   indriyapaccayena 
 paccayo  
         Anidassano dhammo sanidassanassa ca anidassanassa 
 ca dhammassa        
         Sanidassano ca       sanidassanassa  ca       purejātapaccayena paccayo  
           Nahetuyā pañca                 napurejāte cattāri  
           nārammaṇe cattāri                 napacchājāte pañca  
           nādhipatiyā pañca                 sabbattha pañca  
           nānantare pañca                 nasampayutte pañca  
           nasamanantare pañca            navippayutte cattāri  
           nasahajāte pañca                 no atthiyā cattāri   
           na aññamaññe  pañca            nonatthiyā pañca  
           nanissaye cattāri                 novigate pañca  
           na upanissaye pañca            no avigate cattāri

 ṭighā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo

         Arūpī dhammo rūpissa  dhammassa

 paccayo

                           Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
         Rūpī dhammo rūpissa dhammassa sahajātapaccayena 
 paccayo       āhāra   indriya paccayena paccayo  
         Rūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa ārammaṇa         
 sahajāta   upanissaya   purejāta paccayena paccayo  
         Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa ārammaṇa   sahajāta   upanissaya   kammapaccayena paccayo  
         Arūpī dhammo rūpissa dhammassa sahajāta   pacchājātā   kammapaccayena paccayo   
         Arūpī dhammo rūpissa ca arūpicca ca dhammassa 
 sahajāta   kammapaccayena paccayo  
         Rūpī ca arūpi ca dhammā rūpissa dhammassa sahajāta   pacchājāta   āhāra   indriyapaccayena paccayo  
         Rūpī ca arūpī ca dhammā arūpissa dhammassa sahajāta   purejātapaccayena paccayo  
           Nahetuyā satta                 na aññamaññe cha  
           nārammaṇe satta                 nanissaye cha  
           nādhipatiyā satta                 na upanissaye satta  
           nānantare satta                 napurejāte satta       
           nasamanantare satta                  saṃkhittaṃ         
           nasahajāte cha                  namagge satta

                                 XIV  
                           ĀSAVA DUKAṂ   
                                Anulomaṃ   
         Āsavaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca āsavo dhammo uppajjati 
 hetupaccayā  
      Kāmāsavaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhāsavo avijjāsavo  Diṭṭhāsavaṃ 
 paṭicca kāmāsavo avijjāsavo  Avijjāsavaṃ paṭicca kāmāsavo diṭṭhāsavo   Bhavāsavaṃ paṭicca avijjāsavo  Diṭṭhāsavaṃ paṭicca avijjāsavo   Ekekamhi  cakkaṃ kātabbaṃ   
         Āsavaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca no āsavo  dhammo uppajjati 
 hetupaccayā  
      Āsavaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā  khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ 
 ca rūpaṃ  
         Āsavaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca āsavo ca no āsavo ca 
 dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā  
      Kāmāsavaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhāsavo avijjāsavo sampayuttakā 
 ca khandhā  cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ        cakkaṃ 
 bandhitabbaṃ   
         No āsavaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca no āsavo       
      No āsavaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ       pe       dve       pe       
                                                                            K   B  and S  omit second and third sentences  
   S  ekakamhi  R  ekekampi  
   S  has nāsav  nearly always  occasionally no āsav   
      R  has nvāsav   
   R  āsavasampay   here only  
   B  sampayuttakañ ca khandhaṃ

                         Āsavadukaṃ  
 Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca vatthu  vatthuṃ paṭicca 
 khandhā  ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ       pe       mahābhūte

                                 XX  
                           SAṂYOJANA DUKAṂ  
         Saṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano dhammo 
 uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ  paṭicca diṭṭhisaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ  Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca sīlabbataparāmāsasaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ   Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ 
 paṭicca mānasaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ  Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ  Paṭighasaṃyojanaṃ 
 paṭicca issāsaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ  Paṭighasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca macchariyasaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ  
 Paṭighasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ  Mānasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca bhavarāgasaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ  
 Bhavarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ  Vicikicchāsaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ   
         Saṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nosaṃyojano dhammo 
 uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Saṃyojane paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
         Saṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano ca nosaṃyojano ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā  
      Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhisaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ sampayuttakā ca khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca 
 rūpaṃ        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ        
                                                                            S  omits this sentence  
   S  omits  
   B  adds avijjasaññojanaṃ paṭicca vicikicchāsaññojanaṃ  
      S  and K  omit both sentences

 mahābhūtaṃ       pe       mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ

 uppajjati hetupaccayā

 saṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā

 bandhitabbaṃ

 nosaṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā

 tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  dve

                           Nahetupaccayo                
         Saṃyojanasampayutto ca

 tayo khandhā  dve       
         Saṃyojanavippayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā        tīṇi   
         Saṃyojanasampayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā        ekaṃ   
         Saṃyojanasampayuttaṃ ca saṃyojanavippayuttañ ca 
 dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo uppajjati 
 adhipatipaccayā  
      Saṃyojanasampayutte khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca 
 cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ        saṃkhittaṃ   
           Hetuyā nava                      vipāke ekaṃ  
           ārammaṇe cha                      āhāre nava  
           adhipatiyā pañca                 indriye nava  
           anantare cha                      jhāne nava  
           samanantare cha                 magge nava   
           sahajāte nava                     sampayutte cha  
           aññamaññe cha                     vippayutte nava  
           nissaye nava                      atthiyā nava   
           upanissaye cha                  natthiyā cha   
           purejāte cha                      vigate cha  
           āsevane cha                      avigate nava  
           kamme nava  
         Saṃyojanasampayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā

 moho

 moho

 yāva asaññasaṭṭā

           napacchājāte nava                 nonatthiyā tīṇi  
           nāsevane nava                     novigate tīṇi

           napurejāte cha                 navippayutte cattāri  
           napacchājāte nava                 nonatthiyā tīṇi  
           nāsevane nava                     novigate tīṇi

 pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati  jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ

                      Anantaravāro                     
         Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanavippayuttassa

      Sahajātādhipati           khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo  
         Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo       
      Ārammaṇādhipati  sahajātādhipati  Ārammaṇādhipati  
    dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ garuṃ katvā 
 paccavekkhati  pubbe suciṇṇāni        jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā       
 Ariyā maggā       phalaṃ       nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa  abhipatipaccayena paccayo  Sahajātādhipati    saṃyojanavippayuttādhipati       
         Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo       
      Ārammaṇādhipati    dānaṃ        katvā assādeti abhi 
 nandati   taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati  diṭṭhi uppajjati  
 pubbe suciṇṇāni       jhānā       cakkhuṃ       pe

                                 XXIII  
                 SAṂYOJANO CEVA SAṂYOJANIYA DUKAṂ   
         Saṃyojanañ ceva saṃyojaniyañ ca  dhammaṃ paṭicca 
 saṃyojano ceva saṃyojaniyo ca dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhisaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ        cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ   
         Saṃyojanañ ceva saṃyojaniyañ dhammaṃ paṭicca 
 saṃyojaniyo ceva no ca saṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Saṃyojane  paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
         Saṃyojanañ ceva saṃyojaniyañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca 
 saṃyojano ceva saṃyojaniyo  ca saṃyojaniyo ceva no ca 
 saṃyojano ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā  
      Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhisaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ sampayuttakā ca khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca 
 rūpaṃ        cakkaṃ   
         Saṃyojaniyañ ceva no ca saṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca 
 saṃyojaniyo ceva no ca saṃyojanaṃ dhammo       
      Saṃyojaniyañ ceva no ca saṃyojanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ 
 paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  dve       
  paṭisandhi yāva mahābhūtā

   So also R  Cf p       n     
   S  has ending in ā here only  R  omits ca between  jano 
      and dhammā throughout

      Saṃyojaniyañ ceva no ca saṃyojanaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca

                            XXVIII

         Nīvaraṇavippayutto       nīvaraṇasampayuttassa       
      Purejātaṃ     cakkhuṃ       vatthuṃ assādeti abhinandati  taṃ ārabbha rāgo diṭṭhi vicikicchā uddhaccaṃ domanassaṃ uppajjati  Vatthu nīvaraṇasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo

 kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo  Pacchājātā nīvaraṇasampayuttā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo  
           Hetuyā cattāri                 kamme cattāri

           āsevane dve                      avigate satta

                                 XXXVI  
                 NĪVARAṆO CEVA NĪVARAṆIYA DUKAṂ   
         Nīvaraṇaṃ ceva nīvaraṇiyaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nīvaraṇo 
 ceva nīvaraṇiyo ca  dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Kāmacchandanīvaraṇaṃ paṭicca thīnamiddha   uddhacca   
 avijjānīvaraṇaṃ        Evaṃ sabbe gaṇanā vibhajitabbā nīvaraṇadukasadisā  Ninnānākaraṇā Āsavadukasadisā    
         Nīvaraṇo ceva nīvaraṇiyo dhammo nīvaraṇassa ceva 
 nīvaraṇiyassa ca dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo  
      Nīvaraṇā ceva nīvaraṇiyā  ca hetū sampayuttakānaṃ 
 nīvaraṇānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo  
         Nīvaraṇo ceva nīvaraṇiyo ca dhammo nīvaraṇiyassa 
 ceva no ca nīvaraṇassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo  
      Nīvaraṇā ceva nīvaraṇiyā ca hetū sampayuttakānaṃ 
 khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo  
         Nīvaraṇo       nīvaraṇassa ceva       no ca nīvaraṇassa ca dhammassa       
      Nīvaraṇā        khandhānaṃ nīvaraṇānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca       
         Nīvaraṇiyo ceva no ca nīvaraṇo       
      Nīvaraṇiyā ceva no ca nivaraṇā hetū         paṭisandhi

                                 XLII  
                      PARĀMĀSO CEVA PARĀMAṬṬHA DUKAṂ   
         Parāmāsañ ceva parāmaṭṭhaṃ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca 
 parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Parāmāsaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  
         Parāmaṭṭhañ ceva no ca parāmāsaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca 
 parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso

 paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  dve 
        paṭisandhi  yāva ajjhattikā mahābhūtā

 ceva parāmaṭṭho ca

         Parāmaṭṭhañ ceva no ca parāmāsaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca 
 parāmāso ceva parāmāṭṭho ca parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca 
 parāmāso ca       
      Parāmaṭṭhañ ceva        khandhā parāmāso ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca        dve

                            XLIII  
            PARĀMĀSAVIPPAYUTTA PARĀMAṬṬHA DUKAṂ   
         Parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭhaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca 
 parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭho dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā  
      Parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭhaṃ  ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca 
 tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ  dve       
         Parāmāsavippayutta aparāmaṭṭhaṃ  dhammaṃ paṭicca 
 parāmāsavippayutta aparāmaṭṭho dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā        saṃkhittaṃ  yathā cūḷantaraduke lokiyadukaṃ 
 evaṃ kātabbaṃ  Ninnānākaraṇaṃ   
            PARĀMĀSAVIPPAYUTTA PARĀMAṬṬHA DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ  
                                                                            R   yuttaṃ parā   
   K  repeats formula    
      K  NOTE  Ito paraṃ Parāmāso ceva parāmāsasampa     yutta dukassa vibhaṃgo amhākaṃ potthake pi  Sīhaḷapot     thake pi na dissati  Parāmāsaduka parāmāso ceva parā     maṭṭhaduka parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭhadukāni pi Sīha     ḷapotthake na paññāyanti  Etāni amhākaṃ potthake  Pāḷina     yānusāren eva sodhitāni
